Adonques puet il hardiement ovrer, et toutevoies il me semble que mues vaut li laissier.	Then he can hardly work, and still it seems to me that it is better to leave it.
dou cautere de pleuresin	against cauterizing the pleura or lung tissue
Li ancien dirent que on doit faire a pleuresin cauteres de racines d’aristologe, et en teil maniere:	The ancients said that one must perform cauterization on the lungs using roots of aristolochia, and in this manner:
pren une racine d’aristologe longe, la plus grant que tu poras troveir, et soit seche, et soit ausi grosse et ausi longe comme tes dois;	Take a root of aristolochia as long as you can find, the largest possible, and let it be dry, and let its thickness and length be that of your two fingers;
et la moille en oile, et l’emprens au feu, et cauterize I cautere entre la forcele et lou col, et II petis cauteres un poc en dessendant en la partie qui est desoz la barbe;	and mix it with oil, and apply it to the fire, and perform the cauterization between the shoulder and the neck, and perform two small cauterizations slightly descending on the area beneath the beard;
et II cauteres entre la quinte coste et la sisime, en declinant derrier un poc;	and apply cauterization between the fifth rib and the sixth, declining backwards a little;
et I cautere emmi le pis, et I autre sus l’estomac, et I entre II espaules, et II as II costez dou pis defuers le cautere qui est entre II espaules;	and apply one cauterization in the chest, and another on the stomach, and one between the shoulders, and two on the sides of the chest opposite the cauterization which is between the shoulders;
et ne presser mie ta main, ains fai apertement ausi com en odorant.	and do not press with your hand, but make it open as if in a fragrance.
Et dirent aucun ancien que aucun home usent de cautere de feir semblant a I raseur, et l’eschaufent et le mettent entre les costes, tant qu’il vient a cel aposteme;	And certain ancients said that no man should use the fire cauterization similar to a razor, and they warmed it and put it between the ribs, until it comes to that abscess;
et saut fuers li dolor, si com nos avons dit en l’aposteme dou foie.	and the pain will disappear, as we have said in the case of the abscess of the liver.
Mais en cestui ovraige est paour ou li malaides muert maintenant, ou fistule i vient qui ne puet estre sanee.	But in this work there is fear that the patient will die now, or a fistula will come which cannot be healed.
de la mice	of the worm
Quant tu cures la maladie de la mice de ceu que nos avons dit as divisions des cures, et il ne profite mie, adonques i afierent III manieres de cautere que tuit sont boin.	When you treat the disease of the knee that we have spoken of in the divisions of treatments, and it does not benefit from them, then there are three manners of cautery that are good.
Desquelz li une maniere si est que tu faices III cauteres, ou IIII, en lignant selonc la longor de la mice, selonc la figure dou cautere dou foie que nos avons dit devant;	One of the manners is that you make three or four cauteries, applying them along the length of the knee, according to the shape of the cautery of the foot that we have spoken of before;
et n’apresser mie ta main a tout le cautere, et soit li malaides sovins sor son dos;	and do not press your hand on the entire cautery, and let the patient be seated behind his back;
et une autre maniere de cautere si est que tu eschaufe le cautere qui a II ners, si com nos l’avons mostreit en la dislocation de l’espaule;	and another manner of cautery is that you heat the cautery that has two nerves, as we have shown in the dislocation of the shoulder;
et lieve le keur qui est endroit la mice, ou li coutes dou malaide vient devers senestre, et soit li elevations dont tu lieves le keur selonc la keur, selonc la longesce dou cors, et li cautere soient selonc la largesce dou cors.	and lift the heart which is near the knee, or where the cold of the patient comes from the left side, and let the elevation that you lift the heart be according to the heart, according to the length of the body, and the cautery be according to the width of the body.
Aprés i boute les II ners enflamez tant que li keurs soit perciez de l’autre part, et puis trai fuers le cautere, et ensi en i avra IIII.	After that, inflate the two nerves as much as the heart is perceived from the other side, and then apply the cauterization, and thus in this way there will be four.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize a tot le cautere a III ners.	And if you see that it is necessary to cauterize all three nerves.
Aprés le cure quant il a geteit porriture par lonc tens, et ce vaut mues que li autre des cures devant dites.	After the treatment when it has been acquired by long tension, and this is more useful than the other treatments mentioned before.
de ydropisie	of dropsy.
Cautere ne vaut a ydropique, fors c’a la maniere qui est apelee «asclytes».	Cauterization is not suitable for someone with dropsy, except in the manner that is called "ascarides" or "ascites" being referred to as  «asclytes» likely meaning ascites, a condition of dropsy.
Quant tu la cures selonc les manieres que nos avons dit en divisions, et ta cure ne profite mie, adonques covient il que tu li faices IIII cauteres entor la boude, et I sus l’estomac, et un sus le foie, et I sus la mice, et II derrier le dos sus l’espinee, et I endroit le pis;	When you treat it according to the methods that we have mentioned in divisions, and your treatment is not beneficial, then it is necessary that you make four cauterizations around the navel, and one on the stomach, and one on the liver, and one on the spleen, and two behind the back on the spine, and one on the right side of the chest.
et soit li cauteres bien pres de l’espés dou keur.	and let the cauterization be well applied to the thickness of the scar.
Aprés laisse le cautere aovert por giter porriture lonc tens, et ne lassier mie la cure dou malaide aprés le cautere;	Afterwards, leave the cauterized area uncovered for a long time to drain the purulence, and do not hinder the healing of the wound after the cauterization;
et sanation se hasterait, et seront ensamble les II ententions avec l’aide de Deu.	and the healing will hasten, and the two intentions will be joined together with the help of God.
Li forme dou cautere por le ventre soit li clavile que nos avons devant mostreit;	The shape of the cauterization on the abdomen is the clavele that we have previously shown;
et cil por le dos soit olivaire, selonc ceu qu’il est ci devant mis.	and that which is for the back should be olive-shaped, according to what has been set forth before.
de l’enfleure des piez	of the swelling of the feet
Quant li piez sont enflez a celui qui est ydropique, et sont plain d’awe citrine, il covient que tu cauterizes sus le dos dou piet entre l’auriculaire et l’anulaire;	When the feet are swollen in one who is dropsical, and are full of watery citrine, it is necessary that you cauterize on the back of the foot between the thumb and the little finger;
et lieve ta main avec le cautere sens torner.	and lift your hand with the cauterization without turning.
Et n’entrer mie trop em parfont, ensi sarrait fuers li awe citrine, et soit li cauteres selonc cest forme:	And do not enter too deeply, thus would be the exterior of the citrine area, and let the cauterization be according to this form:
Aprés fai sus II jambes II cauteres en chescune jambe a la pointe dou cutellaire;	After that, apply on both thighs two cauterizations, one on each thigh at the tip of the culellatier area;
et soit li cauteres dou lonc, l’un desoz le genoil devant et l’autre defuers, enmi la jambe;	and let the cauterizations be from the length, one of them beneath the knee in front and the other behind, on the middle of the thigh;
et laisse les cauteres aovers longement sens curer, que li awe en isse;	and leave the cauterizations to burn for a long time without covering, so that the area becomes dry;
aprés le cure des autres cures que nos avons dit.	after the treatment of the other treatments that we have mentioned.
de la menoison	of the meniscus
Quant solution de ventre vient de froidor et de moistor, tant que li vertus retentive et digestive qui est ou stomac et en l’intestine est afleboie, et ne puet estre curez par manieres de cures;	When a looseness of the belly comes from cold and moisture, so that the retaining and digestive virtue which is in the stomach and intestines becomes weak, and cannot be cured by methods of treatment;
et tu vois le malaide bien soffrant et de fort vertut, si fai I grant cautere sus l’estomac selonc ceu qu’il en a parleit ci devant ou cautere de l’estomac, au cautere circule;	and you see the patient suffering and of strong virtue, make the great cauterization on the stomach according to what has been spoken of before, or the cauterization of the stomach, in circular cauterization.
et IIII cauteres entor la boude subtilz a tout I cautere clavile subtil, et II cauteres sus les hainches.	and four subtle cauterizations around the navel for every subtle cauterization of the spine, and two cauterizations on the hips.
Et se tu vois les moistors habundans et le malaide soffrant, se li fai cautere sus le poignil, et I cautere sus chaicun yle, et II petis cauteres sus l’estomac delez le grant, car li cure est profitans quant il i a bone aide.	And if you see the muscles abundant and the patient suffering, make a cauterization on the nail, and one cauterization on each heel, and two small cauterizations on the stomach near the navel, for the treatment is profitable when it has good aid.
de la cure des emorroydes	of the treatment of hemorrhoids
Quant les emorroydes sont ou fondement, ou une ou plusors, et sont ancienes et sont de grosses humors froides et moistes corrumpues, et sont curees si com nos avons dit en divisions, et il ne profite mie, si fai cauteres:	When the hemorrhoids are in the foundation, or one or several, and are ancient and are of gross cold and moist humors corrupted, and are curable as we have said in divisions, and it does not profit unless cauterizations are made:
III sus l’espine dou dos, celi qui est tout defuers desoz almecdate poc et poc en triangulant, et I cautere desoz la boude II dois;	On the spine of the back, there is a cauterization which is all deformed and rough, little by little in a triangular shape, and the fire cauterization is on the navel for two fingers;
et se tu penses que ses estomac soit refroidiez, et li viande ne cuise, et on voit enfler la faice, adonques li faice on I grant cautere sus le stomac, si com il est devant dit, et I autre sus le foie, et I autre sus la mice a tout le cautere clavile;	and if you think that his stomach is cooled, and the food does not digest, and one sees the face swollen, then one applies a large cauterization on the stomach, as has been said before, and another on the liver, and another on the spleen with all the cauterizations being applied;
et laisse le cautere overt lonc tens.	and let the cauterization remain on for a long time.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	After the treatment, leave it alone until it is healed.
de la charnositeit qui est nommee «thelul»	of the weakness which is called "thelul
Quant tu copes althelul, si eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et puis le met tout embraseit sus cel althelul copeit;	When you cut into the callus, heat up the cauterization that seems suitable, and then apply it all burnt on the cut callus;
et i laisse tant ta main que li cauteres viegne a la naissance de la voine, de coi li sans cort;	and let your hand be so that the cautery iron comes to the birth of the vein, from which the blood flows.
fai ceu une fois ou II, et s’il i a mout d’althelul, si cauterize chaicun si com nos avons dit;	Do it once or twice, and if there is much of the humour, then cauterize each one as we have said;
aprés les cure d’oignemens profitans tant qu’il soient sanez;	after the treatment of profitable members as long as they are healthy;
et se tu cauterizes d’un cautere grant sus alchatim, si avra plus grant aide.	and if you cauterize with a large cautery on the Achilles tendon, it will have more benefit.
de plaie mal curee	of a wound poorly treated
Quant li malaides ne puet soffrir tailleure ne overture, que nos raconterons en son leu, si vient teil maladie que ne puet estre sanee fuer que par cautere.	When the patient cannot bear cutting or surgical opening, which we will discuss in its proper place, then comes a disease that cannot be cured except by cautery.
Quant a aucun vient fistule, et est enveillie et giete porriture et moistors corrumpues, si la doies prover a tot une tente subtil, et garde que tu saiches a tot la tente combien elle a de parfont.	When to any comes fistula, and it is inflamed and irritated by purulent matter and corrupted humours, then examine thoroughly with a subtle touch, and take care that you know the entire depth of the fistula.
Aprés eschaufe le cautere qui semble I raseur, et le boute en la fistule selonc la quantiteit que li tente i est entrée, et rencomence lou cautere tant que cil cors porris et corrumpus soient ars, une fois, ou II ou III, selonc la quantiteit de som besoing;	After applying the cautery that seems to raise the hair, and put it in the fistula according to the quantity that the tendon has entered, and renew the cautery as long as those rotten and corrupted bodies are burned, one time, or two, or three, according to the quantity of the sore's need.
et te warde d’ardre lé nerf qui sunt enqui, et des grans voinnes.	and protect the nerves that are in danger, and the large veins.
se li fistule vait au cors de la vesie et a l’intestine, si te warde de ces leus, et ne faire ceu fuers que en leu charnut, et pense qu’ele n’est mie persans;	if the fistula goes to the body of the bladder and to the intestine, protect those places, and do not make those sores that are in the flesh raw, and think that it is not a perforating.
aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez, et se li leus est saielez, et les matieres sont ostees lonc tens, adonc saiches que li leus est sanez entierement;	after curing the flesh as long as it is healthy, and if the sores are suppurating, and the matters are thrust out for a long time, then consider that the sore is entirely healthy.
et se les matieres ne sont ostees, saiche que li leus est troez, et corrumpus li os au font;	and if the matters are not thrust out, think that the sore is rotten, and the bone at the bottom is corrupted.
et ensi com un de ces que nos dirons en son leu.	and thus like one of these things that we will tell about in its place
de la maladie des reins	of the disease of the kidneys
Quant dolor de froit vient as rains, et de grosse ventositeit, et ne prent talant de femme, adonc covient il que tu li fais cautere sus les rains d’une part et d’autre au cautere clavile que nos avons devant dit;	When pain of cold comes to the kidneys, and of great swelling, and does not take the shape of a woman, then it is necessary that you perform cauterization on the kidneys on one side and the other with the clavicle cauterization that we have previously mentioned;
et se nos le cauterizons em mileu, si avra III cauteres en ligne, et se feront plus grant aide.	and if we perform the cauterizations in the middle, there will be three cauterizations in a line, and they will be of greater aid.
de la vessie	of the bladder
Quant li vessie est mole et foible de froit et de moistor, si que li malaides retient l’urine, adonc li fai cautere en la partie defuers sus la vessie, la ou encomencent li poil dou poignil, et I a destre et I a senestre, et soit chescuns cauteres si lons com li nous d’un poce;	When the bladder is weak and cold from moisture, so that the patient retains urine, then perform cauterization on the outer part above the bladder, where the hairs of the pubic area begin to grow, and to the right and to the left, and let each cauterization be as long as a finger;
et li fais I cautere defuers le dos, ou II se tu en as besoing;	and have them apply the cautery on the back, or if you are in a need of it;
et soit li cauteres clavile selon la forme devant dite.	and let the cauteries be applied to the collarbone according to the previously mentioned form.
de la marris	of the marrow
Quant li marrix est froide et moiste, et ne laisse mie por ceu a concevoir, et les flors sont corrumpues et lor termines tarde;	When the marrow is cold and moist, and does not allow for this reason to conceive, and the flesh is corrupted and their terms are delayed;
et quant elles vienent, si sent grant dolor:	and when they come, there is great pain:
adonques covient il c’on li faice III cauteres entor la boude, si com nos avons dit ou cautere de la vessie, et II cauteres defuers le dos;	then it is necessary to have three cauteries made around the belly, as we have said regarding the cautery of the bladder, and two cauteries on the back;
et soit li cauteres clavile, si com nos avons dit.	and let the cauteries be applied to the collarbone, as we have said.
de la hainche	of the thigh
Quant les moistors viscouses dessendent a la boiste de la hainche, et por ceste cause si se muet de son leu, et li signes est que li cuisse est plus longe que li autre quant on le mesure ensamble;	When the viscous humors descend to the box of the thigh, and for this reason it moves from its place, and the sign is that the thigh is longer than the other when one measures them together;
et est trovez li leus dou departement vuis, si covient que tu cauterizes le malaide sus la boiste de la hainche a I cautere semblant au cercle, et seigne devant le leu entor la boiste si com elle torne, si que li boiste soit dedens le cercle;	and it is found that the limbs of the department are visible, so it is necessary that you cauterize the patient on the box of the flank to a cautery similar to the circle, and sign in front of the limb around the box as it turns, so that the box is within the circle;
et si soit li cauteres telz com cil dont on a cauterizeit le stomac.	and if the cauteries are such that one has cauterized the stomach.
Et se cist cauteres ne t’est presens, se li fai III cauteres de l’olivaire grans, et soit li cauteres ausi parfont com tous li keurs;	And if these cauteries are not present, make three cauteries of the large olive tree, and let the cauteries be as deep as all the hearts;
et le cure tant qu’il soit sanez.	and heal it until it is healthy.
de la dolor de la hainche	of the pain of the flank
Quant dolor vient en la boiste de la hainche, et c’est de froidor et de moistor, et li malaides est curez de ceu que nos avons dit en la division et li cure ne vaut, et li maladie est anciene:	When pain comes in the box of the flank, and it is from cold and moisture, and the patient is cured of what we have said in the division and the cure is not effective, and the illness is ancient:
adonc covient il que tu purges le malaide des grosses humors de pilules fetides, ou autres pilules bones semblans.	Then it is necessary that you purge the patient of thick foul humors of stinky pills, or other similar bad pills.
Aprés li fai cautere;	After you have done the cauterization;
et li maniere dou cautere si est selonc II manieres:	and the manner of doing the cauterization is according to two methods:
c’est a savoir ensamble medicines ardans, et cautere de feu.	that is to say, applying burning medicines together, and cauterizing with fire.
Cautere de feu si est selonc mout de manieres, desquelz li uns est telz:	Cauterization with fire is according to many methods, of which one is the following:
que tu cauterize sus la boiste de la hainche III cauteres triangulalz selonc ceste forme, et i fai bone profunditeit et grant, et ait entre chaicun cautere d’espaice la groissece d’un doi, et soit li cauteres olivaire;	that you cauterize on the box of the ankle three triangular cauterizations in this form, and make them deep and large, and have between each cauterization a space the thickness of a finger, and let the cauterizations be olive-shaped;
aucune fois fait on cautere en mileu sus lou chief de la hainche, por coi il en i a IIII selonc ceste forme:	sometimes one does a cauterization in the middle on the head of the ankle, because there are four according to this form:
Et se tu vues, si le cauterize au cautere dou cercle que nos avons devant dit en la dislocation de la hainche;	And if you see that the cautery of the circle which we have previously mentioned regarding the dislocation of the thigh;
mais fai en teil maniere que li cercles conteigne toute la hainche, et tous li espés dou keur soit ars.	but make it in such a way that the circles contain the entire thigh, and all the parts of the heart are raised.
Et c’est li maniere c’on fait en sciatique, quant li dolor tient en la hainche, et ne parvient mie jusc’a la cuisse ne jusc’a la jambe.	And this is the way one treats sciatica, when the pain is in the thigh, and does not reach either the knee or the leg.
Et s’ele vient jusc’a la cuisse et la jambe, se li fai II cauteres lai ou li malaides dit que li dolor li tient, et I cautere desus la cheville IIII dois, a la partie senestre un poc;	And if it reaches the knee and the leg, then make two cauteries there where the patient says that the pain is, and one cauterization above the ankle four fingers, on the left side a little;
et soit li cauteres cutellaire, et soit arse li espesseté dou keur;	and let the cauteries be applied with caution, and let the parts of the heart be raised with artistry;
et se li malaides sent que li dolor s’estende jusc’a dois dou piet ou pres d’enqui, se le cauterize la ou il sent la dolor III poins ou IIII au cautere qui est apelez «poins».	and if the patient feels that the pain extends to two fingers or near the navel, then cauterize where he feels the pain three points or four at the cauterization which is called "points".
Et se mestiers est, se li en fai plus;	And if it is a trade, then one does more of it;
et se il seit que li dolor soit desoz le genoil vers la cuisse, se li fais cautere au cautere cutellaire ou circulaire, et te done bien garde en tous tes cauteres que tu n’i lassier mie tant le cautere que tu brules les ners et les grans arteres, et que tu ne faices au malaide plus grant nuisance et contraction.	and if it is known that the pain is below the knee towards the thigh, then perform cautery with a circular or ring-shaped cautery iron, and take great care in all your cauteries that you do not leave the cautery so long that you burn the nerves and the large arteries, and that you do not cause the patient greater nuisance and contraction.
Et je meisme ai veus plusors qui ont fait cautere sus la cheville dou piet, et li lasserent tant que li jambe fut toute enflee, et li piez ausi, et fut perciez et corrumpus toz li piez.	And I myself have seen many who have performed cautery on the leg near the foot, and left it so long that the leg became completely swollen, and the foot as well, and was pierced through and corrupted all the way to the foot.
Aprés une solution de ventre dont il ot la mort.	After a intestinal rupture from which he got death.
Et se li dolors est en II parties ensamble, fai cautere en l’une et en l’autre, selonc ceste maniere.	And if the pains are in two places together, perform cautery in one and in the other, in this manner.
Et li saige dirent en la cautere de la hainche, de coi ci est li maniere, fai I tel fer et soit au chief ausi gros com uns nauvillon de dacte, ou un poc moins, et soit par entrechetres et soit des l’un entrechetres jusc’a l’autre d’espaice la quantiteit d’un nou de poce;	And the wise men said in the cautery of the thigh, that this is the manner, make the iron tool and let it be as thick as a nutmeg seed, or a little less, and let it be notched and let one notch go into another with the space of a thumb;
et soient li entrechetres aovers de II pars, et soient aussi comme noez, et i ait I mainche de fer bien fait;	and let the notches be open on both sides, and let them also be like nuts, and let the iron hand be well made;
et c’est li forme:	and this is the form:
Et soit eschaufez tant qu’il soit toz rouges et giete senteles, et puis le mette on sus la boiste de la hainche malaide, et soit tornez sus lou sain costeit;	And let it be heated until it is entirely red and let the patient feel its heat, and then apply it to the diseased thigh, and let it be turned around the sore area;
et lou cauterize une fois I cautere reont et lou laisse III jors;	and let the cautery be applied once and let it stay for three hours;
et puis fai emplaustre de burre, et laisse la plaie aoverte lonc tens;	and then make a plaster of butter, and let the wound stay covered for a long time;
aprés la cure d’oignement tant qu’il soit sanez.	After the treatment of the injury as long as it is healthy.
Albucasim dit que nos usons poc de cest cautere por la paor de son regart, et se voions poc qui en usent;	Albucasim says that we use little of this cautery because of the danger of its application, and few see those who use it;
et toutevoie ceu est des boins cauteres, qui le puet soffrir, et lai ou il s’afiert.	and nevertheless these are good cauteries, which one can endure, and where they are beneficial.
Li cauteres de medicine ardant si est que tu faices I estrument a entrechetres en coi dessende li marge de la porte, et soit d’arain ou de fer a une paroit longe, et en la hautece ait II nous, et ait entre chaicun la quantiteit de la groissece d’un doi;	The medical cauteries are such that you make the instrument to insert between the lips of the wound, and it should be of copper or iron with a long edge, and in height two nails, and between each one the quantity of the thickness of a finger;
et soient overt defuer et desus, et se joignent ensamble selonc ceste forme:	and are open at top and bottom, and join together according to this form:
Aprés met sus la boiste de la hainche au malaide gisant sor suin costeit sain, et apresse ta main mout sus la boiste de la hainche;	After that put on the bandage of the thigh to the patient sitting on his healthy side, and press your hand much on the bandage of the thigh;
aprés giete entre les II cercles de l’awe chaude qui soit chaufee au feu I poc, et li laisse une houre dou tens, et soffre li malaides la chalor et l’arsure de li.	After the injury between the two circles of the warm water that has been heated by the fire a little, and let it be for an hour of ten, and the patient suffers from heat and burning of it.
Car il i trueve mordication ausi com de feu;	For he finds mortification as if from fire;
et quant li mordications iert passee, se lieve ta main avec l’estrument et leve la hainche d’awe douce, et laisse ensi III jors, et met sus burre tant que ceu qui est noir de l’eschaudure soit osteit;	and when the mortification has passed, raise your hand with the instrument and lift the edge of the warm water, and let it be for three hours, and put on a poultice as long as that which is black from the scab falls off;
et lou laisse III jors que porriture en istrait;	and let it be for three hours that the pus comes out in a stream;
et ceu serait li derriene aide aprés le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	and this would be the last aid after the treatment of unctions as long as he is healthy.
Et se li dolor s’est estendue jusc’a la cuisse ou jusc’a la jambe, se li fai I estrument que teigne awe selonc ceu que tu as fait en la hainche igaument;	And if the pain has spread to the thigh or to the leg, have made an instrument that holds water according to what you have done on the injured limb;
et c’est li maniere de l’awe chaude, et je l’ai escripte ou traitier de la rectification de medicine.	and it is the manner of the hot water, and I have written it in a treatise on the correction of medicine.
Pren alcali et chaulz vive, autant de l’une com de l’autre, et les broie ensamble, et les met en I nuef pot.	Take alkaline substance and living lime, as much of one as of the other, and grind them together, and put them in a new pot.
ou il ait I petit pertuis defuer se que li pointe d’un raisor i puisse entreir;	or it has a small hole made so that the point of a razor can enter;
et met desor celui pot I autre pot bien plombeit, et met sus alcali et chalz et awe douce sus, tant qu’il en i ait I doi desus les poudres cant tu l’avras bien preingte a ta main;	and put that pot into another well-plugged pot, and put on it alkaline substance and lime and sweet water, as much as you will have the powders well ground when you have grasped it with your hand;
et le laisse ensi tant qu’il en dessende awe ague et chiece ou pot plombeit, puis pren toute cele awe, et la giete sus chalz et sus alcali si com devant.	and let it be so until the water descends and the pot is unplugged, then take all that water, and pour it on the lime and on the alkaline substance as before.
Et lors si sera mout ague et est aministree en mou d’ovraiges de medicine et en cauteres d’autres membres.	And then it will be very sharp and is administered in many medical treatments and in cauterizations of other limbs.
Car elle fait auteil oevre com feus, et si a autres medicines dont on cauterize bien la hainche ensi com tesisie et miel anacardi et chalz avec savon, toutes ces choses mellees ensamble.	For it performs the work of fire, and if with other medicines that one cauterizes well the ankle thus as thesis and meal anacardi and chalk with soap, all these things mixed together.
Et Galiens nos raconte une cure dont uns hons fut curez de la dolor de la hainche et de la voine sciatique, et lou loe mout, et dit que on n’i fist autre cure, et qu’il en fut sanez a une soule fois quant on ot fait ceste cure, et il se fut baigniez si com il l’enseigne ci aprés.	And Galen tells us of a cure in which a man was cured of the pain of the ankle and of the sciatic vein, and he loved it much, and said that no other cure was made, and that he was healed at once when this cure was done, and he bathed himself as he teaches here afterwards.
Et dist en teil maniere que tu preignes dou litargire vert fres et sec, et le broie mout avec I poc de graisse, et met sus la hainche et sus la cuisse et sus la jambe ou la dolor tient, et la lie;	And says in such manner that you take green fresh and dry litharge, and crush it much with a bit of grease, and put it on the ankle and on the thigh and on the leg where the pain is, and bind it;
et li laisse III houres et par la quantiteit que li malaides ne sente plus l’arsure.	and let it be for three hours and by the quantity that the patient does not feel the burning anymore.
Et puis le fai entrer ou bain tant que li cors li soit un poc arousez, et lou fai entrer ou lit, et li dolor s’en ira toute et sera sanez.	And then make him enter into a bath until his body is somewhat warmed, and make him enter into bed, and the pain will go away entirely and he will be healthy.
Et saiches que nuls ne doit user de cautere de telz medicines, se ceu n’est aprés l’evacuation de cors.	And be aware that one should not use cauterization of such medicines unless it is after the evacuation of the body.
Et Dyascorides dist que quant li voine sciatique est cauterizee de fiens de chievre, si i aide mout;	And Dyascorides says that when the sciatic vein is cauterized with a fiery cautery, it helps a great deal;
et doit estre fais li cauteres en teil maniere.	and the cauteries should be done in the same manner.
Prenez lainne et la beurez d’oile vielz, et metez sus la fossete qui est entre le pouce dou piez et l’autre qui est apelez foscile.	Take the wool and the extract of old oil, and apply it to the fissure which is between the hollow of the foot and the other which is called the heel.
Aprés pren fiens de chievre sec, et l’empren a feu tant qu’il soit charbons, et lou met sus la laine, et le laisse tant qu’il soit estains;	Afterwards take dry cauterizing iron, and heat it in fire until it becomes charcoal, and apply it to the wool, and let it stay until it is cooled.
et refai encor ensi, et ne cesser de faire ensi tant que tu penses par sens qu’il viegne jusc’a la hainche, et que li dolor soit cessee;	and redo this again, and do not stop doing this as long as you think it is necessary until it comes to the thigh, and that the pain be eased;
et cist manieres de cautere est apelez «cautere de chievre».	and this type of cauterization is called "cauterization of the lip".
de la dolor dou dos	of the pain in the back
Quant dolor vient au dos, ou par cheoir ou de percussion ou par trop grant evacuation, ou par semblans de matiere espandue froide, a nule de ces semblances ne vaut cauteres, fuer que a celi qui vient de infusion de froide matiere.	When pain comes to the back, either by falling or by percussion or by too great evacuation, or by similar things of cold matter spread, none of these things is worth cauterization, except for that which comes from an infusion of cold matter.
Il covient c’aprés ceu que li malaides est voidiez de pilules fetides ou d’autres semblans, que on li faice sus lou dos, lai ou li dolor tient, trois lignes signies d’enche, et en chescune ligne V cauteres ou plus selonc la vertut et la quantiteit que li malaides puet soffrir;	It is necessary after that, that the patient be treated with foul-smelling pills or other similar things, that one apply to their back, there where the pain is, three lined marks of incision, and in each line five or more cauterizations according to the virtue and quantity that the patient can suffer;
et soit fait li cauteres selonc le cautere qui est apelez «poins»;	And let the cauterization be done according to the cauterization that is called "poins".
et se tu vues, fai III cauteres ou IIII au cautere clavile moien selonc ceste forme:	and if you see it, do three or four cauterizations on the middle clavicle according to this form:
Maintes fois vient ceste maladie as petis enfans, et li signes de l’encomencement si est qu’il ont estroite alainne quant il se lievent, et paor;	Many times this disease comes to little children, and the signs of the affliction are that they have a constricted arm when they lift themselves, and fear;
et tu trueves en la derriene espinee dou dos et en nous l’apparance qui vient sus les autres espinees.	and you will find in the upper part of the spine of the back and in the appearance that comes from the other vertebrae.
Quant tu vois ceu et tu le vues curer, si le cauterize au cautere de celcle selonc ceste forme.	When you see this and you consider it to be cured, then cauterize it with the cauterization of that member according to this form.
Si que li cautere porpreigne chescune partie de l’espinee egaument.	Thus the cauterization affects each part of the spine equally.
Et se tu vues, si cauterize entor l’espinee au cautere poignant II lignes ou III, et soient li poins pres l’uns de l’autre.	And if you see it, then cauterize around the spine with the cauterization that pricks two or three lines, and let the points be near one another.
Aprés cure le leu tant qu’il soit sanez selonc ceu que nos avons dit, et warde que tu n’amenistrer cautere en gilbositeit qui soit en spame de nerf.	After curing the injury as long as it is healthy according to what we have said, and beware that you do not apply cauterization in a place where there are nerves in danger of being damaged.
de la dolor des jointes	of the pain of the joints
Quant dolor de jointes sunt de moistors que sont espandues a chaicun membre dou cors, et quant dolor vient em piez, que li mire apelent «podagre» proprement, et quant elle est de froide cause et cures de medicines ne la puent curer, si est curez par cauteres en teil maniere:	When pain in the joints comes from moistures that are spread to each member of the body, and when pain comes in the feet, which the physicians call "podagra" properly, and when it is from a cold cause and cures of medicines cannot cure it, then it is cured by cauterization in such a manner:
fai li mout de cauteres entor la jointure dou piet, et soit li cauteres olivaire selonc ceste forme:	Make many cauterizations around the joint of the foot, and let the cauterization be olive-shaped according to this form:
Et s’il i a besoigne que tu poignes sus la faice dou piet, se li fai cautere a tot le cautere c’on claime «point».	And if there is a spot where you prick on the face of the foot, then make a cauterization at the entire area that one calls a "point".
Et se les dolors viegnent jusc’a genous et as autres jointures, et ceu avient maintes fois, se li fai cautere sus chaicun genoil III cauteres ou IIII de chescunne partie, a tout le cautere olivaire;	And if the pains come near the knees and other joints, and this happens many times, then one should perform cauterization on each knee three or four times, with olive oil for all the cauterizations.
et se tu as mestier de plus, si en fai plus, mais n’i tenir mie ta main fuers que tant que li espés dou keur soit ars.	And if you are a master of many things, do more, but do not hold back your hand more than necessary so that the pressure of the instrument is gentle.
Et se les dolors dessendent jusc’a genoil et au dos, se li aministre le cautere que nos avons dit en son chapistre.	And if the pains descend near the knees and to the back, administer the cauterization that we have spoken of in its chapter.
Et se les dolors sunt as mains, si fai poins entor le foscile II lignes;	And if the pains are in the hands, then make points around the wrist two lines;
et s’il remaint point de dolor as dois, si fai poins sus chescune jointe et sus lou poil de la main;	and if there remains a point of pain in the fingers, then make points on each joint and on the hair of the hand;
et se les dolors vienent jusc’as coutes ou jusc’as espaules, si cauterize chescune partie, et fai boin governement au malaide et penre medicines.	and if the pains come near the ribs or near the shoulders, then cauterize each part, and make good governance for the patient and think of medicines.
Car se tu li fais boin governement et tu purges fleume, si sera saneis a l’aide de Deu.	For if you make a good government for yourself and purge the phlegm, you will be healed with the help of God.
de la routure dou syfac	of the rupture of the spleen
Quant routure vient en angres, et li bouelz dessendent as coions et c’est novelement, si covient que quant tu lou vues curer, qu’il ne menjuce mie celui jor;	When a rupture comes to the entrails, and the bowels descend to the groin and it is new, then it is necessary that when you want to cure it, that you do not touch that member today;
et qu’il use choses qui laichent lou ventre, si que li fiens dessende de son ventre;	and that he uses things which lighten the stomach, so that the feces descend from his stomach;
aprés le fai seoir sus son dos entre tes mains, et li comande qu’il teigne son alaine tant que li boueil soient repairiet, et les ramoinne a tes dois, et seigne d’enche desoz la routure sus l’os dou poignil, et a tout un signe que soit semblans a la moitiet d’un cercle a desus dou cors;	after that, make him sit on his back between your hands, and instruct him to hold his belly as long as the bowels are being repaired, and put them back in place, and sign from below the rupture on the bone of the hip, and make a sign that is similar to half a circle above the body;
puis eschaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	then heat the cautery according to what its form is:
tant qu’il soit blans et qu’il giete senteles.	As long as they are bald and throw away sensations.
Puis ramoine les bouels a lor leu;	Then reset the intestines to their place;
et li ministres teigne sa main sus qu’il ne retornent arrier;	and let the assistants hold his hand so that it does not turn back;
et oevre bien les cuisses au malaide, et met desoz lui I cussin et I serjant sus les cuisses, et I autre sus lou pis qui li teigne les mains;	and open well the thighs of the patient, and put a cushion under him and a servant on the thighs, and another on his chest who holds his hands;
puis met le cautere sus lou signe a tout ta main, et lou tien droit et lou tien tant que tu ateignes l’os, et se tu ne l’ateins la premiere fois, si le rencomence encor une autre tant que tu viegnes jusc’a l’os;	then put the cautery on the sign with your whole hand, and hold it straight and firm until you reach the bone, and if you do not reach it the first time, then recommend it again another time until you come to the bone;
et te warde subtilment que li boueil ne saille quant tu fais lou cautere;	and beware subtly that the intestine does not protrude when you perform the cautery;
que tu ne le brulasses;	that you do not burn it;
et que par ceu li malaides ne muere, ou autre malz.	and that because of this the patient does not die, or have other ills.
Et saiches que quant tu ne viens jusc’a l’os au cautere, tes ovraiges ne vaut rien.	And know that when you do not apply the fire to the cautery, your work is worth nothing.
Et covient que li cauteres des enfans soit subtilz selonc la mesure d’ous, et des grans gens aussi grans selonc lor mesure;	And it is fitting that the cauterization of children be subtle according to the measure of their ears, and for large people also large according to their measurement;
aprés III jors cure lou leu dou cautere de burre tant que li eschaudure soit ostee;	after three days cure the limb from the cautery of tar until the scab is removed;
aprés le cure d’autres oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez, et gise li malaides XL jors sus son dos tant que li plaie soit bien soudee;	after curing other ulcers until it is healed, and let the patient lie on his back for 40 days while the wound is well dried;
et covient que ses norrissemens soit lassatis longement, si que li boueil ne saillent quant il se preigdra d’aler en chambres.	and it is fitting that his bandages be tied loosely, so that the belly does not swell when he gets up to go to the chambers.
Et aprés XL jors, quant il se voudra lever, se li amenistre une faixe bien faite, et la porse XL autres jors;	And after 40 days, when he wants to get up, a well-made splint should be applied to him, and the poultice for another 40 days;
et ait boin repos, qu’il se travaille poc et se warde de trop grant repletion de boivre et de mengier, et de trop haut braire;	and let it have good rest, so that it works little and guards against too great a filling of drinking and eating, and of too high a fever.
et quant il fait cest enseignement si est sanez entierement.	and when he makes this teaching then is health entirely.
Et je dirai ci aprés la cure de taillier en son chapistre.	And I will speak afterwards of the treatment for cutting in its chapter.
de la routure dou ventre	of the rupture of the belly
Quant routures vienent en autres ventres et sont connisans, et tu vues qu’elles ne croissent plus, se li fai I cautere dou cautere reont selonc sa quantiteit, et soit ars li tiers dou keur;	When ruptures come in other bellies and are connected, and you see that they do not grow more, then have made the cautery of the cautery repeated according to its quantity, and let it be the third of the heart;
aprés le cure selonc ceu que nos avons dit;	after the cure according to what we have said;
et aucun des anciens ont dit c’on le doit cauterizer au cautere a III angles selonc ceste forme:	and none of the ancients have said that one should be cauterized with a cautery at three angles according to this form:
mais signe premier le leu d’enche et fai une ligne per la largesce desus la routure, et une autre defuers, et main ta main emmi a tout le cautere clavile.	but first mark the limit of the flesh and make a line across the width above the rupture, and another below, and hold your hand in the middle to all the cauterized claw.
Mais li premiers cauteres est plus legiers et muedres.	But the first cauterizations are lighter and more moderate.
de dolor anciene en aucun membre	of pain in old age in any member
Quant dolor vient en aucun membre, ou de cheoir ou de ferir, et cele dolor tient lonc tens, et li cure de medicine n’i vaut, adonc covient qu’il soit cauterizeis au cautere qui est apelez «poins», et soit li cauteres selonc la longesce dou membre et la petitece et sa foibleteit et sa vertut et sa location de torcions et de sa dolor.	When pain comes in any member, from a fall or a blow, and that pain holds for a long time, and the cure of medicine is not effective, then it is necessary that it be cauterized with a cautery which is called "poins", and let the cautery be according to the length of the member and its smallness and weakness and its virtue and location of torsions and of its pain.
s’il est sanez dou premier cautere, c’est bien;	if it is healed by the first cauterization, that's good;
se ceu nom, recomence I autre cautere sus celui, car teilz costume est qu’il se doit muer au membre que li est prochiens, por coi il covient que tu faices les cauteres tant que li malaides soit saneis.	if that does not work, recommend another cauterization on that one, for such is the custom that it must change in the member which is affected, therefore it is necessary that you do the cauterizations as long as the patient is not healed.
de meselerie	of mixture
Li meseil sont aidiet aucune fois par cautere par grant aide, et meismement li maladie que vient de la putrefaction de fleume et de melancolie.	The doctors are helped many times by cautery with great aid, and similarly the disease that comes from the putrefaction of phlegm and melancholy.
Cant tu la vues cauterizer, pren warde se li maladie est au comencement, et s’ele est curee selonc ceu que nos avons dit en la division, et ne dessent ne ne demoure, et tu doutes que li corruption ne porpreigne tout le malaide, adonques li fai V cauteres sus lou chief:	When you see the need to cauterize, beware that the disease is at its beginning, and if it is curable according to what we have said in the division, and does not descend nor remain, and you doubt that the corruption will not spread throughout the whole disease, then make a cautery on the head.
I emmi le chief a nouf, et l’autre vers lou front a la fin des chevous;	Put one cautery on the head at the navel, and the other towards the forehead at the end of the eyebrows;
et II sus les II cornes, et I derrierre sus le haiterel;	and two on the two horns, and one behind on the occipital bone;
et i laise tant ta main que li cauteres viegne jusc’a l’os, et tant que les escorces en issent fors si que les vapors des grosses humors s’en puissent issir;	and let your hand be such that the cautery reaches just to the bone, and as long as the scorchings issue forth so that the vapors of the gross humors can come out;
et le cauterize sus la mice selonc ce qu’il est devant.	and the cauterization on the mouse according to what is in front of it.
Et se li meselerie est partout esparse;	And if the mixture is scattered all around;
et elle pert manifestement, si covient que tu lou cauterizes de ces cauteres que nos avons dit ou chief, et I cautere en som lou neis, et II cauteres sus l’espinee dou col, et VI cauteres sus l’espinee dou dos, et I grant sus la crupie et I autre delez, et II sus les II espaules;	and it falls manifestly, then you should apply the cauterization of these cauterizations that we have mentioned in the head, and one cauterization on the nape of the neck, and two cauterizations on the spine of the neck, and six cauterizations on the spine of the back, and one large one on the thigh, and another below it, and two on the shoulders;
et II sus les coutes, et II sus les tendrons dou pis, et I sus chascune jointe des mains et des piez, et sus les fosses des mains;	and two on the hips, and two on the tendons of the feet, and one on each joint of the hands and of the feet, and on the palms of the hands;
et te warde des ners que sunt sus lou derrien calcant, que tu ne les bruler;	and beware of the nerves that are on the rear calf, that you do not burn them;
et aucune fois fait om cautere sus l’os dou poignil, et I autre sus l’os de l’estomac, et I autre sus lou foie.	and sometimes make a cauterization on the bone of the finger, and another on the bone of the stomach, and another on the liver.
Et saiches que quant plus i fais de cautere, plus li fais d’aide, et mues li profite;	And know that the more I do of cauterization, the more it aids him, and moves him to profit;
et saiches que li malaides ne sent point de dolor au cautere si com li sain le sentent, por ce que li cors est ja toz corrumpus.	and know that the patient does not feel any pain from the cauterization as much as they think they do, because their body is already completely corrupted.
Et covient ke li cautere soient grant et petit selonc les membres et les jointures, selonc ceu que vos lou troverez en manieres des fers.	And it is necessary that the cauterizations be large and small according to the limbs and joints, according to what you will find in the manners of the cases.
Aprés cure lou leu de farine de veces avec miel et autres cures tant qu’il soit saneis.	After the cure, anoint the limb with flour of wheaten bread and honey and other treatments until it is healed.
Quant enfleure vient en aucun membre et est curee par medicines et oiles et emplastres, et il n’est mie sanez, adonques li fai cauteres sus le membre selonc la grandour et la petitece dou membre;	When inflammation comes into any limb and is treated with medicines and oils and plasters, and it is not healed, then have cauterizations on the limb according to its size and smallness.
et soit li cauteres un poc entrans en l’espés dou keur;	and let the cauterization be a little within the thickness of the skin;
puis le cure d’oignemens tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then heal the joints as long as they are healthy.
Et aucune fois fait on cautere et a la main et au piet et au dos, a l’issue dou nerf que muet le membre, et ensi si est ostee li enfleure;	And sometimes cauterization is performed on the hand and on the foot and on the back, at the exit of the nerve that moves the limb, and thus the swelling is reduced;
et toutevoie ne s’en entremette nuls s’il n’est conoissans des membres et des issues des ners movans lou cors.	and in no way should one interfere unless they are knowledgeable about the limbs and the exits of the nerves moving the body.
de albaras	of paralysis
Quant li maladie qui est apelee «albaras» est enveillie, et li engien de medicine n’i valent rien, adonques le cauterize d’un cautere un poc parfont, selonc la quantiteit de l’espés dou keur, tant que li blenchour soit ostee, et soit muee sa color;	When the disease called "paralysis" has invaded, and the engines of medicine are of no value, then cauterization with a cautery is performed somewhat deeply, according to the quantity of the thickness of the skin, until the whiteness is removed, and its color is changed;
puis le cure de farine de veces et de lentilles avec oile roset et foilles de plantain, et sanc de colon et sanc d’alondre, de chescun une partie;	Then heal with flour of roots and with lenses using rose oil and leaves of plantain, and blood of colchicum and blood of almonds, each a part;
et soit mellez tout ensamble, et soit liiez d’un drapel, et soit aers au leu tant qu’il soit sanez.	and be wrapped altogether, and be tied with a cloth, and be raised to the level as long as it is healthy.
li cure de chancre par cautere	The treatment of cancer by cauterization
Quant chancre vient au comencement, et tu lou vues arrester, si le cauterize au cautere qui semble I cercle, tout entor au tour dou chancre.	When cancer comes at the beginning, and you want to stop it, then cauterize with a cauterizing iron which seems a circle, all around the tumor of the cancer.
Et toutevoie li saige dirent que on faice cautere ausi au mileu dou chancre;	And all the wise men said that one should do cauterization in the middle of the cancer;
et toutevoie ceu ne me semble mie boin, car je redous que il ne soit ulcerez et corrumpus, et je l’ai ja veut avenir aucune fois;	and yet this does not seem good to me, for I fear that it will be ulcerated and corrupted, and I have already seen it happen many times;
et plus droituriere chose est qu’il soit cauteriés entor, au cautere qui est apelez «circule», si com nos avons dit en mout de cauteres.	and the most rightful thing is that it be cauterized around, with the cauterizing iron that is called "circle", as we have said in many cauterizations.
de l’enfleure qui ne puet meurer	of the swelling that cannot be measured
Quant aucuns ait une maladie qui est apelee «adubelati», et elle tarde de meurer ou por la superfluiteit qu’ele fait ou por l’eaige dou malaide quant il est decrepites (c’est a dire trop vielz) et il a poc de sanc, ou por lou tens;	When some people have a disease called «adubelati», and it slows down their urine or because of the excess that it produces or because of the pain of the disease when it is decrepit (that is to say too old) and they have little blood, or because of their tension;
et tu la vues haster de meurer:	and you hasten the stoppage of urinating:
adonques le cauterize entor de mout de petis cauteres en poignant;	then one cauterizes within many small cauterizations by pricking;
aprés le laisse ensi.	after that, leave it thus.
Car elle se hastera de meureir.	For it will hasten the stoppage of urinating.
Et se tu la vues percier a tout le cautere, si chaufe le cautere de coi ci est li forme:	And if you hasten to pierce all the cauterization, heat the cauterizer from where its form is:
Et met ta main en mileu de cele maladie qui est apellee «adubelati» tant que li cauteres ait perciet lou keur, et soit telz li cauteres que li malaides lou sente defuers en teil maniere que li cours de la porriture soit alegis.	And put your hand in the middle of that disease which is called «adubelati» until the cauterizations have pierced the heart, and let the cauterizations be such that the patient feels better in some manner so that the course of the disease is alleviated.
Aprés le cure tant qu’il soit sanez parfaitement.	After the treatment as long as it is perfectly healthy.
li cure dou feu par fer	The treatment of fire by means of iron.
Une autre maniere de maladie i a qui est apelee «corrodens», et n’est autre chose que une mengeson de membre, car ele menjut les membres ausi com li feus les leignes seches.	Another kind of disease is what is called "corrosion", and it is nothing other than a wasting away of a member, for it wastes the members just as fire does the dry wood.
Se tu vois ceste maladie en leu qui puisse soffrir cautere ensamble feu, adonques eschaufe les cauteres clavile mout petit et grant, selonc ceu qu’il covient au leu ou li maladie est;	If you see this disease in a patient who can suffer cauterization with fire, then heat the cauterizing irons very little and greatly, according to what is needed for the patient or where the disease is.
aprés le cauterize de toutes pars tant que tu erraiche toute la corruption, et nen remaigne rien de li, que tout ceu qui est corrumpus ne soit osteit.	After the cauterization of all parts as long as you eradicate all the corruption, and do not leave any of it, that all that is corrupted be removed.
Et puis le laisse III jors, et met sus les leus cauterizez soffre broiet avec oile tant que les eschaudures dou feu soient ostees, et toute li corruption.	And then let it be for three days, and apply to the cauterized limbs a soothing balm made with oil, until the burns from the fire are removed, and all the corruption.
Aprés lou cure d’oignemens engendrans char.	After the treatment of painful gums produces fever.
Et se tu vois aprés III jors que chars saine ne naisse, c’est boin;	And if you see that after three days a healthy gum does not grow, it is good;
et se ceu non, si rencomence le cautere sus ceu qui est demoreit des leus corrumpus.	and if it does not, then repeat the cauterization on that which has remained of the rotten flesh.
Et ceste mengeson est aucune fois esteit curee de medicine ague en leu de cautere de feu;	And this swelling has sometimes been cured by sharp medicine instead of fire cauterization;
mais toutevoie cautere de feu est de plus grant aide, et j’ai ja dit la cure de la medicine ague en la division:	but nonetheless fire cauterization is of greater aid, and I have already spoken of the cure by sharp medicine in the division:
pren la quant tu en as mestier.	take what you have in your profession.
des porrelz qui vienent as piez	of stones that come to the feet
Mout de fois avient que as piez par defuers naist une maladie qui est apelee «clos» selonc nostre entencion, et est une grosse chose fautree qui blece lou piet.	Many times it happens that in the feet by default arises a disease which is called "cloches" according to our intention, and is a large false body that blocks the foot.
Et li cauteres de ceste maladie si est selonc II manieres.	And the cauterizations of this disease are in two ways.
C’est a savoir cautere de feu, et cautere d’aigue chaude.	It is to know about cautery of fire, and cautery of hot water.
Cautere de feu si est que tu eschaufe I cautere cheveit ausi com est une penne de vouteul, et soit fait de boin fer a la mesure qu’il puisse porpenre le clou de toutes pars, et qu’il i ait subtilz marges;	Cautery of fire is that you heat I, the cautery iron, as is a pen of hollow metal, and be made of good iron to the measure that it can pierce the nail from all sides, and that it has subtle edges;
aprés le met tout chaut sus lou clou, et torne ta main tot entor le clou tant qu’il viegne au font dou clou;	after you put all hot on the nail, and turn your hand all around the nail until it comes to the bottom of the nail;
et lou laisse ensi III jors tant qu’il encomence giter porriture;	and let it stay thus three hours until it induces a purulent discharge;
puis li fai un emplaustre de malves savaiges broiies avec seil, et laisse l’emplaustre sus toute la nuit, et li clous cherra et sera desracinez de ses racines.	then make a plaster of wild mallows bruised with oil, and let the plaster stay on all night, and the nail will fall out and be disrooted from its roots.
Puis cure le leu d’oignement enjanrant char tant qu’il soit sanez.	Then treat the wounded limb by anointing with heat until it is healthy.
Et s’il sont convertit par defuers lou cors, et maintes fois avient et en mains et em piez, si covient que tu i amenistres cautere d’aigue chaude;	And if they are affected by various humors in the body, and often occur in the hands and feet, then it is necessary that you apply cauterization of warm water.
et est en teil maniere:	and it is in a similar manner:
pren une cainne d’arain ou de fer, ou une penne de vouteul, et met sus lou clou et l’althelul, c’est asavoir porrelz verrues;	Take a chain of iron or of steel, or a needle of a spearhead, and put it on the nail and the elbow, that is to remove warts;
et met la cainne sus si qu’ele porpreigne tout entor, puis i met un poc d’awe chaude, et retien bien ta main, et presse ta main en tornant si que li marge de la cainne viegne a la racine dou clou, et puisse trover l’aigue chaude voie parfonde jusc’a la racine;	and put the chain on it so that it embraces all around, then put a little warm water, and hold your hand firmly, and press your hand turning it so that the margin of the chain comes to the root of the nail, and then find the warm water passing deep to the root;
et soffre li malaides un poc la mordication de l’aigue chaude une houre;	and let the patient suffer a little the burning of the warm water for an hour;
puis le laisse ensi, et il se derracinera tous a tout ses racines.	then leave it thus, and it will uproot itself completely along with all its roots.
Ensi fai un aprés autre, tant que tu esraiches toz ces qui sont au cors, puis les cure des oignemens qui engenrent char.	Thus do one thing after another, as long as you treat all those who are in the body, then cure the wounds that produce fever.
li cure dou trembler	the cure for trembling
Quant aucuns tremble de froidor de ners, ou de fievre quartaine ou d’autre, si covient que tu li faices IIII cauteres ou IV sus l’espinee dou dos, I cautere entre chescune espinee;	When some people shiver from cold or from nerves, or from quartan fever or other, it is suitable that you do four cauterizations or four on the spine of the back, one cauterization between each vertebra;
et I cautere ou pez, et I sus l’estomac au cautere olivaire;	and one cauterization on the foot, and one on the stomach for an olive cauterization;
si laissera lou trembler, et se hastera li santez de la maladie froide.	if it leaves the trembling, and hastens the health from the cold disease.
des pustules puans	of festering pimples
Aucune fois apperent par defuers le cors bathes, ou pustules puans, que vienent de grosses matieres corrumpues.	Some times appear on the body boils, or festering pimples, that come from corrupted thick matters.
si covient au premier quant eles apperent que on faice cautere sus chescun chief de la pustule:	it is suitable at first when they appear that one do cauterization on each head of the pimple:
un cautere subtil de fust de mirte, de coi li pointe soit emprise au feu, ou de racine de aristologe longe, ou au cautere lenticulaire.	A subtle cauterization of the skin with a pointed instrument heated by fire, or with the root of aristolochia longa, or with a lentical cauterizer.
Et aucune fois les cauterize on au comencement quant il aperent, selonc ceste maniere, et il ne puent croistre des enqui en avant, mais est desrompue li superfluitez dont il vienent, et sont sanez;	And sometimes they cauterize at the beginning when it appears, in this manner, and it cannot grow from the wounds beforehand, but is broken up the excess flesh that comes from them, and they are healed;
mais il covient que ceu soit fait aprés l’evacuation de sanc.	but it is necessary that this be done after the evacuation of blood.
quant li artere est copee	when the artery is cut
Maintes fois avient grans decorremens de sanc de l’artere qui est copee a la plaie que vient au pardefuers, ou a l’incision de l’aposteme, ou au cautere dou membre, et as semblans choses;	Many times there are great outpourings of blood from the cut artery that come from the wound in the armpit, or from the incision of an abscess, or from cauterization of a limb, and similar things;
et est mout grief chose d’estenchier.	and it is a very grievous thing to staunch.
Et toutevoie quant ceu avient a aucun, si te haste de mettre ton doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne, et l’estrain mout tant que li sans soit apaisiez desoz ton doi, et que goute n’en isse plus;	And always when that happens to someone, if you hasten to put your second finger on the wound of the vein, and strain a lot so that the blood is calmed beneath your finger, and does not come out anymore;
puis met au feu les cauteres olivaire plusors petis et grans tant qu’il soient tuit rouge;	then put to the fire the olive cauteries many small and large as they are well roasted red;
puis empren I, ou grant ou petit selonc la plaie et lou leu en coi li artere est route, et met le cautere sus cele voine ou tu tiens ton doi, et tien le cautere tant sus que li sans soit restainchiez.	then take I, either large or small according to the wound and the place in which the artery is broken, and put the cautery on that vein where you hold your finger, and hold the cautery as long as the blood is restrained.
Et s’il saut fuers quant tu lieves ton doi desus la voinne, et li cauteres estint, si pren hastivement I autre des cauteres qui sont au feu.	And if it still flows when you lift your finger from the vein, and the cautery is not effective, then quickly take another of the cauteries that are on the fire.
Et ne cesser de faire ceu l’un aprés l’autre tant que li sans soit estenchiez;	And do not stop doing this one after the other until the blood is stanched;
et warde que tu n’ardes lou nerf qui est delez, et que autre malice ne viegne sus lou malaide;	and beware that you do not injure the nerve that is nearby, and that another evil does not come to the patient;
et saiches que quant sans decourt de l’artere, c’on ne lou puet mie bien restenchier meismement quant li artere est grans, se ceu n’est par une des IIII manieres que nos avons dit:	and be aware that when the blood does not flow from the artery, one cannot well restore it, especially when the artery is large, unless it is by one of the four methods that we have mentioned:
ou par cautere, ou par extraction quant ele n’est mie traite, ou par fort liement de fil, ou par medicines mises sus qui ont pooir de restenchier sanc;	or by cauterization, or by extraction when it is not treated, or by strong tightening of a thread, or by medications applied which have the power to restore blood;
et soit liee et estrainte avennament.	and let it be bound and constricted firmly.
Qui i amenistrera restenchement de liier estroitement de drapelz ou de metre choses ardans sus, ou autres semblans choses, se n’i profite se poc non.	For one will not profit from binding a tight bandage or placing warm things on, or other similar things, if not much.
Et se ce avient a aucun et il n’ait mie mire ne medicine present, si doit mettre son doi indice sus la plaie de la voinne si com nos avons dit, et bien estrendre tant qu’il soit restenchiez desus la plaie et desus la voinne;	And if it happens to anyone and he does not have a doctor or medicine present, then he should put his index finger on the wound of the vein as we have said, and bind it well until it is restored above the wound and above the vein;
et ne remuer lou doit, mais lou moille d’awe froide sovent que soit mout froide tant que li sans soit congelez et engrossiez et restenchiez;	and do not move the [affected] part, but rather apply cold moisture often so that it is very cold until the blood is congealed and thickened and restrained;
et faice des enqui en avant ceu dont il a mestier de cauteres et de medicines.	and make inquiries beforehand about what is needed for cauteries and medicines.
Ci encomence li secons livre des cures de taille	In this book the second section deals with the treatments of the thigh
Nos vos avons dit ou premier chapistre toute maladie en coi il covient cautere de feu, ou de medicine ardans, et les oquisons et les causes et les estrumens et les formes des cauteres;	We have said in the first chapter all about the disease for which it is necessary to use fire cauterization, or burning medicines, and the tools and causes and instruments and forms of cauterizations;
et ai mis celui chapistre des lou chief jusc’a piez, et je irai en cest chapistre par celi meisme voie por ceu c’on trueve plus legierement ceu c’on voura.	and I placed that chapter concerning the head down to the feet, and I will proceed in this chapter by the same method because one finds it easier what one desires.
Et ainsois que je encomence ceu, il covient, chier fil, que vos aprenez que en cest chapistre a plus de peril et de paor que ou premier des cauteres, et por ceu il covient plus grant cautele.	And thus I begin with this, it is necessary, dear reader, that you learn that in this chapter there is more danger and fear than in the first one about cauterizations, and for this reason it requires greater caution.
Car en l’ovraige de cest chapistre avient maintes fois evacuation de sanc a l’ovrir la voinne, et a l’incision sus aposteme, et as cures des plaies, et a l’estraction des saiettes, et a l’incision sus la piere, et les semblans choses;	For in the work of this chapter, there is often the evacuation of blood when opening a vein, and incising an abscess, and in the treatment of wounds, and in the extraction of arrows, and in cutting into stones, and similar things;
ou il a doutance et paor, et en vient li mors a plusors.	where there is doubt and fear, and many die.
Et je vos amoneste que vos n’entreprenez folie.	And I advise you that you do not undertake folly.
Car mout de manieres de gens vienent en cures.	For many kinds of people come for treatment.
si vienent de telz qui s’aïrent si avec lor maladie qu’il muerent legierement por la forsenerie qu’il trueve de sa maladie, et de la grandour de son malice;	if there come those who are so accustomed to their illness that they move lightly because of the familiarity they have with their disease, and the greatness of their suffering;
et de ces doit on avoir paor.	and one should be afraid of these.
Et de ces i a qui te done son sens, et dit:	And to this one who gives his opinion, and says:
«atendez, je sui garis»;	wait, I am a leper";
et li maladie est despitouse.	and the disease is contemptible.
Il ne covient mie que vos vos consentez a ces qui vienent a vos qui ont ceste maniere, mais mettez plus grant cusanson en vostre honor qu’en vostre covoitise, et n’ovrez mie folement mais saigement de ceu dont vos estes certain, et dont vos poez avoir pris et los;	It does not matter that you consent to those who come to you with this condition, but put greater consideration in your honor than in your covetousness, and do not open foolishly but wisely regarding that which you are certain of, and that which you can have taken and gained.
et usez de pronostication et de indication en cures de vos malaides a coi salus soit convertie;	and use prognosis and indication in the treatment of your diseases so that health may be converted.
et ceu vos aidera a aquester bone renommee, et gloire, et memoire de loenge.	and this will help you to acquire a good reputation, and glory, and long memory.
Tres chier fil, Nostres Sires vos doint boin entendement et droiture, et se vos vuelle espireir de la sainte inspiration de sa main, amen.	Dearest son, Our Lord grant you good understanding and righteousness, and if you want to aspire to the holy inspiration of his hand, amen.
Or je vos ai ordeneit cest chapistre en devisant par chapistres, selonc ceu qu’il est devant ou chapistre des cauteres, que je vos ai deviseit des le chief jusc’a piez, por ceu que vos trovez plus legierement ceu dont vos avrez mestier.	Now I have ordered this chapter for you by dividing it into chapters, according to what it is before the chapter on cauteries, which I have divided for you from head to feet, so that you find more easily that which you will need.
dou chief plein d’aigue	The head full of anguish
Saiches que ceste maladie vient mout de fois as enfans a l’enfanter, et quant li baille estraint trop fort le chief de l’enfant;	It is known that this illness often comes to infants at birth, and when the midwife holds the head of the infant too tightly;
et aucune fois vient ceu de cause reponue que on ne seit.	and sometimes it occurs without any apparent reason that one knows.
Et je ne vis onques ceste maladie fuers qu’en enfans, et a toz ces que j’ai veus se hastait li mors;	And I have never seen this illness except in infants, and most of those whom I have seen hasten their death;
et por ceu me semble qu’il me vaut mues lassier l’ovraige en teilz cures.	and for this reason it seems to me that it is worth including the treatment in several cures.
Et je vis I enfant de coi li chiés estoit plains d’aigue, et li chief engroissoit chescun jor tant qu’il ne lou pooit sostenir;	And I saw an infant whose head was full of anguish, and the head grew so large every day that it could not be supported;
et crut tant li moistor qu’il fut mors, et ceste moistor si est assemblee desoz l’os sus lou syphac, entre lou keur et l’os;	and the moisture increased so much that it became a tumor, and this tumor is assembled below the bone on the spine, between the heart and the bone;
et li ovraiges si est telz se li moistor est entre lou keur et l’os, et li apostemes est petis, que tu fendes emmi lou chief une fendure large;	and the works are such that the moisture is between the heart and the bone, and the abscesses are small, that you make in the head a wide incision;
et soit ausi longe com II nous, tant que li mostor corre;	and let it be as long as two of us, until the moisture flows;
et vez ci la forme dou spatumile:	and see to the form of the spatula or spoon;
Se li moistor est plus creue, et li aposteme soit plus grans, si fai II fendures en maniere d’une croix, selonc ceste forme:	If the moisture is more increased, and the abscess is larger, then make two incisions in the manner of a cross, according to this form:
Et se li moistor est desoz l’os, et li signes que tu vois les commissures dou chief overtes de chescune partie, et li aigue saut fuer quant tu la presses de ta main au dedens, et ceu ne t’est mie reponut:	And if the moisture is disordered in the bone, and the signs that you see the sutures of the head are open on each side, and the water jumps when you press it with your hand from within, and this does not respond to treatment:
si covient que tu fendes enmi lou chief III fendures selonc ceste maniere:	then it is necessary that you make three incisions in the head according to this manner:
Et aprés l’incision estrai la moistor toute fuers.	And after the incision, extract the moisture entirely from outside.
Aprés estraint les fendures de drapelz et de poudres, et i met vin et oile, et laisse ensi jusc’a cinquieme jor;	After constraining the fractures of bandages and powders, and put wine and oil, and leave them like that until the fifth day;
puis le deslie, et cure la plaie par tentes et par oignemens, et laisse estraindre le chief egaument, et done mengier au malaide viande seche de poc de moistor tant que li membre soit confortez et sanez.	then undo it, and treat the wound with dressings and with anointments, and let the head be constrained, and give to eat to the patient dry food of little moisture until the limb is comforted and healthy.
Et une autre maniere d’incision est que tu regardes ou apert li grandor de l’aposteme, et li assemblé de l’aigue;	And another manner of incision is that you look at the size of the abscess, and the gathering of the pus;
car aucune fois est elle devant;	for sometimes it is in front;
aucune fois derrier;	sometimes it is behind;
aucune fois en destre;	sometimes it is on the right;
et aucune fois en senestre.	and sometimes it is on the left.
Taille donques lai ou li aposteme apert, et l’emplissement de l’aigue, et lou fent selonc ce que tu en as le pooir;	Cut then the place where the abscess appears, and the filling of the pus, and make the incision according to that which you have the power;
et warde que tu ne coper l’artere;	and beware that you do not cut the artery;
et veigne flun de sanc, si que li malaides muere dou decorrement de sanc et de l’evacuation de moistor.	and stop the flow of blood, so that the patient dies from lack of blood and from evacuation of moisture.
de reume	of rheum
Quant il avient a aucun une maladie qui est apelee «catarre» as eulz ou au pis, et li maladie est anciainne, et li cure de medicine ne profite mie, adonques li derraine cure si est li cauteres avec ceu c’on li copera les II arteres.	When there is a disease called "catarrh" in the eyes or in the chest, and the disease is chronic, and the treatment with medicine is of no benefit, then the last resort is cauterization with what one cuts the two arteries.
Il covient donques, cant tu les vues coper, que li malaides faice rere son chief;	It is necessary, then, when you cut the veins, that the patient make his head fall back;
aprés li frotte lou leu d’un drapel aspre tant que les arteres aperent, puis estraingne li malaides son col a tout I drapel;	after rubbing the limb with a coarse cloth so that the arteries appear, then the patient tightens his neck against the entire cloth;
puis regarde ou li voine bait, et li leus de l’une et de l’autre sont aprés les oreilles, et poc sont reponues;	then look where the vein is visible, and the limbs of one and the other are behind the ears, and are slightly raised;
puis signe les leus d’enche, puis cope l’une et l’autre d’un spatumile agut de II pars, tant que li taille veigne jusc’a l’os, et ceu soit par lou large dou chief.	Then mark the limbs from the beginning, then cut one and the other with a sharp spatula on both sides, as far as the vertebrae reaches to the bone, and that which is through the wide wound of the head.
Et se tu vues, boute le spatumile desoz l’artere et la cope au desus, en taillant ausi com II dois au traver.	And if you see, remove the spatula from beneath the artery and cut above, carving just as the two veins across.
Et quant li voinne est copee, si saut li sans en haut continuelment fuers.	And when the vein is cut, then let the blood flow out continuously upwards.
Et se li artere n’apert au sentir, si covient que tu mesures la quantiteit de l’espaice de III dois, puis seigne d’enche et fent jusc’a l’os;	And if the artery does not appear to feeling, then it is necessary that you measure the quantity of the space of three fingers, then mark from the beginning and make until the bone;
et ceu qu’il covient dou sanc mettre fuers si est VI c/, et par aventure un poc plus ou moins, selonc ce que li malaides puet soffrir, et la repletion de l’artere;	and that which is necessary to put blood flowing if it is six and a fraction, and by chance a little more or less, according to what the patient can suffer, and the replenishment of the artery;
puis regarde la plaie:	then examine the wound:
s’il remaint sus l’os point dou syphac, si le cope que apostemes chaus n’i veigne, puis estrain la plaie et lie, et la cure d’oignement tant qu’ele soit sanee.	if it remains on the bone a pointed syphac, if the abscess does not heal, then strain the wound and bind it, and the treatment of ointment until it is healed.
de emigrainne	of emigraine
Quant emigrainne anciaine vient, et catarre agut, por les moistors des larmes et les chalors en temples et sode anciene forsenee et semblans choses, et il est medicinez par manieres de cures de medicine et tout ceu ne li profite mie, si estraions les arteres des temples et lou cauterizons, si com nos avons conteit.	When ancient migraine comes, and sharp caterization, because of the moistures of tears and the heat on the temples and old forehead weakness and similar things, and it is treated by means of medical cures and all that does not profit him, then we cauterize the arteries of the temples and do the cauterization, as we have related.
Et li maniere de l’estraction d’elles si est que li malaides faice rere les poilz de ses temples, et entende a l’artere qui apert en la temple, car elle apert bien par son batement, et est poc reponue fuers que en aucuns homes qui sont trop froit;	And the manner of the extraction of them is that the patient makes to raise the hairs of his temples, and attend to the artery which opens in the temple, for it opens well by its beating, and is hardly found outside in some men who are too cold;
et s’elle est reponue, si estraigne son col li malaides d’aucuns drapelz, puis frote le leu d’aucun aspre drap, et arose le leu d’aigue chaude tant que li artere apere manifestement;	and if it is replaced, then remove the patient's neck from certain bandages, then rub the limb with a coarse cloth, and raise the limb with warm water as long as the artery appears manifestly;
puis pren le spatumile de coi ci est li forme:	then take the spatula of which this is the shape:
puis escorche le cuir legierement tant que tu veignes a l’artere, puis la trai en haut as pinceures, et la depart bien des toiles que sont desoz li de chescune partie;	then scratch the skin lightly until you come to the artery, then pull it up with pincers, and separate it well from the tendons that are attached to each part;
